Its statistics, other than its size and speed, are unchanged. Anything it is wearing transforms with it, but nothing it is carrying does. It reverts to its true form if it dies., While in mist form, the vampire can't take any actions, speak, or manipulate objects. It is weightless, has a flying speed of 20 feet, can hover, and can enter a hostile creature's space and stop there. In addition, if air can pass through a space, the mist can do so without squeezing, and it can't pass through water. It has advantage on Strength, Dexterity, and Constitution saving throws, and it is immune to all nonmagical damage, except the damage it takes from sunlight.</li><li><strong>Legendary Resistance (3/Day):</strong> If the vampire fails a saving throw, it can choose to succeed instead.</li><li><strong>Misty Escape:</strong> When it drops to 0 hit points outside its resting place, the vampire transforms into a cloud of mist (as in the Shapechanger trait) instead of falling <strong>unconscious</strong>, provided that it isn't in sunlight or running water. If it can't transform, it is destroyed., While it has 0 hit points in mist form, it can't revert to its vampire form, and it must reach its resting place within 2 hours or be destroyed. Once in its resting place, it reverts to its vampire form. It is then <strong>paralyzed</strong> until it regains at least 1 hit point. After spending 1 hour in its resting place with 0 hit points, it regains 1 hit point.</li><li><strong>Regeneration:</strong> The vampire regains 20 hit points at the start of its turn if it has at least 1 hit point and isn't in sunlight or running water. If the vampire takes radiant damage or damage from holy water, this trait doesn't function at the start of the vampire's next turn.</li><li><strong>Spider Climb:</strong> The vampire can climb difficult surfaces, including upside down on ceilings, without needing to make an ability check.</li><li><strong>Vampire Weaknesses:</strong> The vampire has the following flaws:, TAG:i The vampire can't enter a residence without an invitation from one of the occupants., TAG:i The vampire takes 20 acid damage if it ends its turn in running water., TAG:i If a piercing weapon made of wood is driven into the vampire's heart while the vampire is <strong>incapacitated</strong> in its resting place, the vampire is <strong>paralyzed</strong> until the stake is removed., TAG:i The vampire takes 20 radiant damage when it starts its turn in sunlight. While in sunlight, it has disadvantage on attack rolls and ability checks.</li> </ul></div>   <hr/> <h6>Actions</h6> <div><ul> <li><strong>Multiattack (Vampire Form Only):</strong> The vampire makes two attacks, only one of which can be a bite attack.</li><li><strong>Unarmed Strike (Vampire Form Only):</strong> <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d20+9' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d20+9');"><strong><strong>+9</strong></strong></a> to hit, reach 5 ft., one creature. It otherwise uses the possessed target's statistics, but doesn't gain access to the target's knowledge, class features, or proficiencies., The possession lasts until the body drops to 0 hit points, the ghost ends it as a bonus action, or the ghost is turned or forced out by an effect like the TAG:spell spell. When the possession ends, the ghost reappears in an unoccupied space within 5 feet of the body. The target is immune to this ghost's Possession for 24 hours after succeeding on the saving throw or after the possession ends.</li> </ul></div>  </div> </div> </div> </div> </td> </tr>     <tr> <td> 3 </td> <td> Skeletons </td> <td> <div id="block-CnfD6TZV" class="monster-block"> <div class="statblock"> <div class="statblock-top-row"> <div><span class="section-label">CR:</span> 1/4 (50 XP)</div> <div><span class="section-label">AC:</span> 13 (armor scraps)</div> <div><span class="section-label">HP:</span>  (2d8 + 4)</div> <div><span class="section-label">Speed:</span> Walk 30 ft.</div> </div> <table class="statblock-table"> <tr><th>STR</th><th>DEX</th><th>CON</th><th>INT</th><th>WIS</th><th>CHA</th></tr> <tr> <td>10 <small>  </small> </td> <td>14 <small> +2 </small> </td> <td>15 <small> +3 </small> </td> <td>6 <small> -2 </small> </td> <td>8 <small> -1 </small> </td> <td>5 <small> -3 </small> </td> </tr> </table> <div> <input class="monster-block-toggle" name="toggle-CnfD6TZV" id="toggle-CnfD6TZV" type="checkbox" onclick="javascript:document.getElementById('block-CnfD6TZV').scrollIntoView();"/> <div id="block-toggle-CnfD6TZV" class="statblock-container"> <ul>   <li><strong>Immunities: </strong> poison</li>   <li><strong>Senses: </strong> darkvision 60 ft.</li>   <li><strong>Alignment: </strong> Lawful Evil</li>   <li><strong>Languages: </strong> understands all languages it spoke in life but can't speak</li>  </ul>   <hr/> <h6>Actions</h6> <div><ul> <li><strong>Shortsword:</strong> <a class="btn-spawn-dice" data-dice='1d20+4' onclick="javascript:window.app.spawn_dice('1d20+4');"><strong><strong>+4</strong></strong></a> to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.
